The International Flag Parade at University Day is a way to show off how many nations are represented at UNT. If you want to show your pride for your nationality, sign up to carry your nation&#039;s flag. Contact the International Center, Marquis Hall 110, at (940) 369-8625 or internationalcenter&#064;unt.edu. Participants are also encouraged to wear something from their countries, whether that is a soccer jersey or a national dress.</p><div class="_5wpt"></div></div><div class="_3x-2"><div
